 i was in Switzerland in those days and was busy completing my book a Brief History of Time
 tabhi mujhe seene main infections hua or phir ye neumonia main badal gaya

 Expressing anger over the acute shortage of teachers in iits, iims and universities, a parliamentary panel asked the government to take steps to fill the vacancies and make the teaching profession more attractive
 ek report main bhaajapa saansad satyanarayan jatiya kii adhyakshata main maanav sansaadhan vikaas par sansad kii sthaayee samiti ne ucch shiksha vibhaag se rictiyon ko bharne kii prakriya tej karne ke liye kaha he
 The committee expressed its anger that many posts were lying vacant in prestigious central universities, newly established universities, state or private universities, iits and iims
 31 sadasyeey panel ne kaha ki gunvatttapurna shiksha ke liye paryaapt sankhya main or yogya shikshak hona jaruri he
 The situation remains grave due to no improvement in the near future
 samiti ne kaha, ‘‘do sambhaavnaaen ho sakati he yaa to hamaare yuva chaatr shikshak ke peshey kii ore aakarshith nahin he yaa bhartee prakriya lambit he or isamen kai prakriyaagat aupchaariktaayen shaamil he
 '' echaradi mantralay ke tahat aane vaale ucch shiksha vibhaag kaa zikr karte huye panel ne kaha ki yah puure desh main ucch shiksha ke kshetra k liye nodel praadhikaran he or use maujuuda rictiyon kii bhartee prakriya tej karne main sakriy bhoomika nibhaani chaiye
 The panel also recommended that faculty members should be encouraged to provide support to the advisory body to make the course of teaching more attractive and they should also be given financial assistance to start their work
 echaradi mantralay ne gat varsh disambar main sansad main bataaya tha ki vibhinn kendriya vishvavidhyalayon main prophessoron ke 1,310 pad khaali pade hai
 In the recently concluded parliament session, HRD Minister Prakash Javadekar had said that most of the vacant posts of teachers in universities and colleges will be filled this year
 tippaniyan It is worth noting that out of total 17,006 posts of teachers in various UGC funded Central Universities, 6,080 posts are vacant since October 1, 2016
 panel ne apni report main chaatro main rojgaar ke kaushal kii kami par bhi chintaa jataayi or sarkaar se is par kadam uthaane ke liye kaha he
 In a report, the Parliamentary Standing Committee on Human Resource Development headed by BJP MP Satyanarayana Jatia has asked the Higher Education Department to speed up the process of filling vacancies
 samiti ne is par gussa jataayaa ki pratishthit kendriya vishvavidhyalayon se lekar haal main sthapit vishvavidhyalayon, rajya yaa nijee vishvavidhyalayon, iaiti or im main kai pad rikt pade hai
 The 31-member panel said that it is necessary to have sufficient number of qualified teachers for quality education
 nikat bhavishya main koi sudhaar naa dikhne se sthiti kaaphi gambhir bani hui he
 The committee said, "there could be two possibilities, either our young student is not attracted to the teacher's profession or the recruitment process is pending and involves many procedural formalities
" ’’ Referring to the Department of Higher Education under the HRD Ministry, the panel said that it is the nodal authority for the field of higher education all over the country and should play an active role in speeding up the recruitment process for the existing vacancies
 panel ne yah bhi sifarish kii ki shikshan ke pesh ko adhik aakshark banane ke liye faikalti sadasyon ko salaahkaari sanstha kii madad dene ke liye protsaahit karnaa chaiye or unhen apana kaam shuru karne ke liye vittiya sahaayta bhi deni chaiye
 The HRD Ministry had told the Parliament in December last year that 1,310 posts of professors in various central universities are lying vacant
 haal hi main sampann sansad satr main echaradi mantri prakaash jaavdekar ne kaha tha ki vishvavidhyalayon or collejon main shikshakon ke zyaadaatar rikt padon ko is varsh bharaa jayega
 The comments gauratlab he ki ujisi poshit vibhinn kendriya vishvavidhyalayon main shikshakon ke kul 17,006 padon main se 6,080 pad ek aktubar 2016 se rikt hai
